Everything you need is to buy a ticket. * * * FACILITY AND FURNISHING * * * 1x Living room - with sofa bed 140cm x 200cm (cold foam mattress on slat bed frame) - (desk) table + chair 1x Bedroom with - bed: 140cm x 200cm with pocket spring mattress - one air bed (100cm x 200cm x 40cm high) for a additional person. 1x Fitted kitchen - equipped with kitchenware, Kettle, Toaster, coffee machine.                       <div data-reactid="417">
                       Crystal clear seas, palm-fringed sandy beaches, historic sites - all this you will certainly not find here in Gostenhof. Instead, we open a guest room with the style of the famous Café "Salon Regina". The apartment will open in December 2012. More pictures will follow when we are finished with the fine work. The apartment we have adapted to the design concept of the café, which is located in the front building. We mix the substance present with objects from the past and of our time. Selected findings with its own history and contemporary design furniture complement each other. For this purpose we equip the apartment with relevant, practical and simply beautiful things. Discover these unexpected details and hopefully you find time to relax on the big, sunny roof terrace. Numerous cafes, bars and galleries invite you to dive in and discover. The apartment is rented as a unit daily to 1 to 2 persons and has a living and sleeping area with 1 double bed and a cozy corner to relax, as well as a fully equipped kitchen and a bathroom with bathtub. There is Wi-Fi available and there is a music system available. We also furnish the apartment with relevant journals, magazines and books. We are centrally located, just 2 metro stations in the city and 4 to the central station. The exhibition area is also easily reached in 14 minutes nonstop. But since it is the most beautiful thing to explore above the ground we offer to our guests free of charge bicyles with a deposit. Properly for stranded-, business-, relaxlooking-, creative-, musical-people. For those who live happiness and love.

                      <div data-reactid="667">
                       Dear Visitor(s)! My 1-room-apt. is located close to the city center in a upper standard neighbourhood, right at the Park called "Wöhrder Wiese". The Metro is right in front of the Apt., so e.g. Nuremberg Messe is within 15 minutes of commute! The city center and one of the biggest movie theaters in Europe is within walkable distance (less than 15 min.). The Apt. is perfect for one guest but comfortably hosts 2. Looking forward to your messages &amp; meeting you!
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="668">
                       The apartment is about 380 square feet and has a balcony. There's a kitchen and a bathroom - all personal! I won't be in the apartment during your stay, so you can feel like you're home! The bed is 6,5 feet long and 5,2 feet wide. Before every arrival, the whole apartment is thoroughly cleaned! I always provide fresh bed sheets and covers as well as enough towels for your stay. If you wish to bring your own stuff, just let me know - of course you can! Toilet paper and other items for daily use are sufficiently provided. The apartment is perfect if you travel alone. Two persons can comfortably stay there. If you wish to bring another person or your pet, let me know! It's located on the first floor. Nonetheless there are about 10 steps to go up - I'm afraid it's not suitable for handicapped. The balcony is directed to the inner courtyard, so it's quiet and you won't hear any noise from the streets.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="669">
                       The apartment is in a high-class neighbourhood close to the Wöhrder Wiese park. It's an absolutely safe area - you don't need to worry about anything here. Right in front of the house there's a café (currently closed), restaurants and a bakery are within closest walking distance. In few minutes of walking you get to the Cinecitta (cinema) to enjoy a movie or start your trip to the inner city! The university and a library are also around. Grocery stores and a laundry shop are close as well.

                     <div data-reactid="1099">
                      <div data-reactid="1100">
                       Das Apartment liegt in einem trendigen Altbau, in dem begehrten Stadtteil Johannis. Es bietet Platz für bis zu 4 Personen hat 3-Zimmer, 56qm, hohe Decken und ist stilvoll eingerichtet. Vollausstattung mit schnellem WIFI, Flatscreen-TV, Spül- und Waschmaschine, Küche, Bad mit Dusche/Wannenkombination.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1101">
                       Stilvoll eingerichtetes und ruhiges Apartment am Rand der Nürnberger Altstadt. In nur 5 min zur Burg - die perfekte Lage für Deine Zeit in Nürnberg! Das 3-Zimmer Apartment ist sehr zentral und verkehrsgünstig, aber dennoch ruhig gelegen. Ich freue mich Euch ein Zuhause mitten in Nürnberg anbieten zu können. Im Apartment können max. 4 Personen wohnen, zusätzlich ist noch ein Babybett möglich. Das gesamte Apartment ist im Januar 2017 neu eingerichtet worden aus einer Mischung von Antiquitäten und moderner Einrichtung. Das Apartment hat einen Flur mit einem Schuhschrank und Garderobe. Das Schlafzimmer ist mit einem Doppelbett (180 x 200) und Kleiderschrank ausgestattet. Antike Möbel und echte Teppiche sorgen im Esszimmer für ein besonderes Flair. Im Wohnzimmer befindet sich eine neue Schlafcouch (140x200) und ein Flachbildfernseher (40 Zoll). Eine modern ausgestatte Küche mit Cerankochfeld, Backofen, Spülmaschine, Mikrowelle und einem großen Kühlschrank mit Gefrierfach bietet alle Möglichkeiten zum Kochen. Außerdem stehen eine Nespresso Kaffemaschine mit Milchschäumer, Wasserkocher und volles Küchenequipement zur Verfügung. Das elegant gestaltete Badezimmer hat Tageslicht, Badewanne, WC und Waschbecken. Außerdem stehen eine Waschmaschine, Föhn, Handtücher und Badeuntensilien bereit. Kostenfreies WLAN. Ein Bügelbrett und Bügeleisen sind vorhanden, Kinderbett und Hochstuhl auf Anfrage.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1102">
                       Das Appartement befindet sich im Erdgeschoss eines Mehrfamilienhauses im Wohngebiet nahe der Nürnberger Altstadt. Johannis ist einer der ältesten Stadtteile Nürnbergs. Studenten, Alt-Eingesessene und Familien sind Deine Nachbarn.                        <li data-reactid="1823"><p data-reactid="1824">My wife and I stayed at Harry's during a trip through Europe by train. It was an easy 7-10 minute walk from the central station (Nuremberg HBF) and we were met by a friend of Harry's who showed us in. The building is in three levels - bar at ground level, record store 2nd floor, and The Nest on the third. It's a great little apartment and the photos were very accurate. The rooms are actually bigger than they appear and were clean, crisp and modern. Harry has gone through a lot of effort to modernise the place and make it a nice space, with magazines, cool artwork, blankets on the sofa, local guidebooks, hotel-like amenties in the bathroom, a solid sound bar, (SENSITIVE CONTENTS HIDDEN) Chromecast on the TV and strong Wifi. We spent almost a whole day being lazy inside and cooked a few meals there too. The kitchen is well kitted out (minus an oven, and a dishwasher but this is easily managed and didn't detract from the stay). Harry is a good guy too - we went to coffee and he gave us sightseeing and restaurant/bar recommendations. We also hung out at his bar on two nights and met all the locals which was really good fun. The nightlife across the street can get a little noisy but out of the 4 nights we had, only once did I pull out some earplugs (that Harry supplies by the bed). His own bar downstairs didn't keep us up at all! Finally, the location is killer! We were 8 or 9 minutes from the Christmas Markets (which is a good thing considering how crowded they get), and you're 30 seconds from the main shopping strip and all kinds of food and drink. The subway is a few minutes up the street and the touristy castle area only 20 mins walk. Overall, we loved staying at Harry's and wished other airbnbs we stayed at during the trip were as set up as this, with such high attention to detail.                       <div data-reactid="1927">
                       Our bright and comfortable studio with 27m² is situated in Nurembergs beautiful historical center. 2014 we renovated it completely and decorated it new. The city center with its sights, shops and restaurants invites you for a stroll around the town.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1928">
                       You want to spend a vacation or business stay in the heart of Nuremberg's Old Town? Then our apartment is the right place for you! It offers all the amenities for a relaxing stay in Nuremberg. A bright living room with oak flooring offers on 27 m² a fully equipped kitchen unit with stove, oven, microwave and dishwasher. Moreover, there is a dining area for 4 persons. The sofa can be converted into a bed for 2 people and invites you to relax. In addition there is a sleeping area with a bed (bed with two new mattresses, which can be converted into a double bed) and a cupboard. A south-facing balcony completes the comfort of this bright space. A small but beautiful bathroom with rain-shower provides the necessary daily freshness before you go on a sightseeing trip or your business meeting. Suitable for(URL HIDDEN)Business and leisure traveler(URL HIDDEN)Long term renters welcom(URL HIDDEN)Non smoking propert(URL HIDDEN)Pets not allowed
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1929">
                       It is located in the heart of the city center: a variety of shops and boutiques invite you to stroll and shop. Several restaurants, bars and cozy pubs are within walking distance. Take time to explore the pedestrian zone as well as the many small alleyways in the old town and let yourself be inspired by its flair. For visitors who are keen on culture: the most important museums of the city of Nuremberg are located in the immediate vicinity of the apartment, as well as the most important sights such as Christkindlesmarkt, Sebaldus-Kirche, Kaiser-Burg or Dürer-Haus etc.
